TL;DR: 该研究通过动态规划求解器分析算术谜题的结构性难度决定因素，发现最小构造中使用的输入值数量是难度的最小充分统计量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究算术谜题游戏中的难度结构决定因素，为自适应学习系统中的数学推理任务难度分析提供理论基础，解决智能练习系统的核心挑战。

Method: 开发精确的动态规划求解器，枚举可达目标并提取最小操作见证；构建超过340万个实例的数据集，通过最小操作数定义难度；分析难度与求解器导出特征的关系。

Result: 基于统计的机器学习模型只能部分预测可解性，但无法可靠区分简单实例；难度完全由少量可解释的结构属性决定，特别是最小构造中使用的输入值数量是难度的最小充分统计量。

Conclusion: 研究提供了透明、计算基础的谜题难度解释框架，连接了符号推理和数据驱动建模，支持可解释的难度估计和原则性任务排序，对自适应算术学习和智能练习系统有直接应用价值。

Abstract: Arithmetic puzzle games provide a controlled setting for studying difficulty in mathematical reasoning tasks, a core challenge in adaptive learning systems. We investigate the structural determinants of difficulty in a class of integer arithmetic puzzles inspired by number games. We formalize the problem and develop an exact dynamic-programming solver that enumerates reachable targets, extracts minimal-operation witnesses, and enables large-scale labeling.
  Using this solver, we construct a dataset of over 3.4 million instances and define difficulty via the minimum number of operations required to reach a target. We analyze the relationship between difficulty and solver-derived features. While baseline machine learning models based on bag- and target-level statistics can partially predict solvability, they fail to reliably distinguish easy instances. In contrast, we show that difficulty is fully determined by a small set of interpretable structural attributes derived from exact witnesses. In particular, the number of input values used in a minimal construction serves as a minimal sufficient statistic for difficulty under this labeling.
  These results provide a transparent, computationally grounded account of puzzle difficulty that bridges symbolic reasoning and data-driven modeling. The framework supports explainable difficulty estimation and principled task sequencing, with direct implications for adaptive arithmetic learning and intelligent practice systems.

</details>


### [196] [Does Structured Intent Representation Generalize? A Cross-Language, Cross-Model Empirical Study of 5W3H Prompting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25379)
*Peng Gang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究验证了基于5W3H的结构化意图表示框架PPS在多语言和多模型中的泛化能力，发现AI辅助扩展的5W3H提示与人工编写的效果相当，结构化表示能改善意图对齐并降低非专家用户使用门槛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证结构化意图表示框架PPS是否能在不同语言和模型中泛化，扩展先前仅针对中文的研究，探索AI辅助界面自动扩展简单提示为完整5W3H规范的效果，以及跨模型输出一致性问题。

Method: 采用5W3H框架的PPS结构化意图表示，在三个语言（中文、英文、日文）和四种条件下进行实验：A)无约束基线，B)简单提示，C)手动编写5W3H，D)AI辅助扩展5W3H。使用三个大语言模型在60个任务上生成2,160个模型输出，分析目标对齐度和跨模型输出一致性。

Result: AI扩展的5W3H提示（条件D）在所有三种语言中与手动编写的5W3H提示（条件C）在目标对齐方面无显著差异，而用户只需输入单句。结构化PPS条件通常减少或重塑跨模型输出方差，但效果因语言和指标而异。非结构化提示表现出系统性双重膨胀偏差：人为高复合分数和人为低表观跨模型方差。

Conclusion: 结构化5W3H表示能改善跨语言和模型的意图对齐和可访问性，特别是当AI辅助创作降低非专家用户的使用门槛时。研究为结构化意图表示在多语言环境中的实用性和泛化能力提供了实证支持。

Abstract: Does structured intent representation generalize across languages and models? We study PPS (Prompt Protocol Specification), a 5W3H-based framework for structured intent representation in human-AI interaction, and extend prior Chinese-only evidence along three dimensions: two additional languages (English and Japanese), a fourth condition in which a user's simple prompt is automatically expanded into a full 5W3H specification by an AI-assisted authoring interface, and a new research question on cross-model output consistency. Across 2,160 model outputs (3 languages x 4 conditions x 3 LLMs x 60 tasks), we find that AI-expanded 5W3H prompts (Condition D) show no statistically significant difference in goal alignment from manually crafted 5W3H prompts (Condition C) across all three languages, while requiring only a single-sentence input from the user. Structured PPS conditions often reduce or reshape cross-model output variance, though this effect is not uniform across languages and metrics; the strongest evidence comes from identifying spurious low variance in unconstrained baselines. We also show that unstructured prompts exhibit a systematic dual-inflation bias: artificially high composite scores and artificially low apparent cross-model variance. These findings suggest that structured 5W3H representations can improve intent alignment and accessibility across languages and models, especially when AI-assisted authoring lowers the barrier for non-expert users.

### [197] [Modernising Reinforcement Learning-Based Navigation for Embodied Semantic Scene Graph Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25415)
*Roman Kueble,Marco Hueller,Mrunmai Phatak,Rainer Lienhart,Joerg Haehner*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个模块化导航组件用于具身语义场景图生成，通过改进优化算法和动作表示来提升在有限动作预算下的探索效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语义世界模型使具身智能体能够超越纯几何表示来推理物体、关系和空间上下文。在有机计算中，这种模型是在不确定性和资源约束下实现目标驱动自适应的关键。核心挑战是在有限的动作预算内获取最大化模型质量和下游有用性的观察。

Method: 研究提出了模块化导航组件用于具身语义场景图生成，通过以下方法改进决策：1) 替换策略优化方法；2) 重新审视离散动作表述；3) 研究紧凑和细粒度的离散运动集；4) 比较原子动作的单头策略与动作组件的分解多头策略；5) 评估课程学习和可选的基于深度的碰撞监督。

Result: 结果显示：1) 仅替换优化算法就能在相同奖励塑造下将SSG完整性相对基线提高21%；2) 深度主要影响执行安全性（无碰撞运动），而完整性基本不变；3) 现代优化与细粒度分解动作表示相结合产生了最强的整体完整性-效率权衡。

Conclusion: 通过改进优化算法和采用更细粒度的分解动作表示，可以显著提升具身语义场景图生成的探索效率和完整性，同时保持执行安全性，为有限动作预算下的语义世界模型构建提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Semantic world models enable embodied agents to reason about objects, relations, and spatial context beyond purely geometric representations. In Organic Computing, such models are a key enabler for objective-driven self-adaptation under uncertainty and resource constraints. The core challenge is to acquire observations maximising model quality and downstream usefulness within a limited action budget.
  Semantic scene graphs (SSGs) provide a structured and compact representation for this purpose. However, constructing them within a finite action horizon requires exploration strategies that trade off information gain against navigation cost and decide when additional actions yield diminishing returns.
  This work presents a modular navigation component for Embodied Semantic Scene Graph Generation and modernises its decision-making by replacing the policy-optimisation method and revisiting the discrete action formulation. We study compact and finer-grained, larger discrete motion sets and compare a single-head policy over atomic actions with a factorised multi-head policy over action components. We evaluate curriculum learning and optional depth-based collision supervision, and assess SSG completeness, execution safety, and navigation behaviour.
  Results show that replacing the optimisation algorithm alone improves SSG completeness by 21\% relative to the baseline under identical reward shaping. Depth mainly affects execution safety (collision-free motion), while completeness remains largely unchanged. Combining modern optimisation with a finer-grained, factorised action representation yields the strongest overall completeness--efficiency trade-off.

### [198] [Retraining as Approximate Bayesian Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25480)
*Harrison Katz*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上模型重新训练被视为常规维护任务，但作者认为需要更理论化的框架来指导重新训练决策，以优化计算资源使用并提高模型治理的可审计性。

Method: 将重新训练视为计算约束下的近似贝叶斯推断，引入"学习债务"概念（连续更新的信念状态与冻结部署模型之间的差距），建立基于决策理论的重新训练策略框架，推导出基于损失函数的阈值触发机制。

Result: 开发出基于证据的触发机制，替代传统的日历调度方式，使重新训练决策更加科学，同时提高治理过程的可审计性。

Conclusion: 重新训练应被视为计算约束下的贝叶斯推断问题，通过决策理论框架可以优化重新训练策略，实现更有效的模型维护和治理。

Abstract: Model retraining is usually treated as an ongoing maintenance task. But as Harrison Katz now argues, retraining can be better understood as approximate Bayesian inference under computational constraints. The gap between a continuously updated belief state and your frozen deployed model is "learning debt," and the retraining decision is a cost minimization problem with a threshold that falls out of your loss function. In this article Katz provides a decision-theoretic framework for retraining policies. The result is evidence-based triggers that replace calendar schedules and make governance auditable. For readers less familiar with the Bayesian and decision-theoretic language, key terms are defined in a glossary at the end of the article.

Abstract: We introduce Voxtral TTS, an expressive multilingual text-to-speech model that generates natural speech from as little as 3 seconds of reference audio. Voxtral TTS adopts a hybrid architecture that combines auto-regressive generation of semantic speech tokens with flow-matching for acoustic tokens. These tokens are encoded and decoded with Voxtral Codec, a speech tokenizer trained from scratch with a hybrid VQ-FSQ quantization scheme. In human evaluations conducted by native speakers, Voxtral TTS is preferred for multilingual voice cloning due to its naturalness and expressivity, achieving a 68.4\% win rate over ElevenLabs Flash v2.5. We release the model weights under a CC BY-NC license.

### [200] [R-C2: Cycle-Consistent Reinforcement Learning Improves Multimodal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25720)
*Zirui Zhang,Haoyu Dong,Kexin Pei,Chengzhi Mao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RC2：通过强化学习框架利用跨模态不一致性作为学习信号，通过强制跨模态循环一致性来提升多模态模型的推理准确性


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态模型在处理同一概念的视觉和文本表示时经常产生矛盾预测，这种跨模态不一致性通常被标准投票机制掩盖，但作者认为这种不一致性实际上提供了丰富的自然学习信号

Method: 提出RC2强化学习框架，通过强制跨模态循环一致性来解决内部冲突：要求模型执行反向推理、切换模态，并通过前向推理可靠地重建答案，从而获得密集的无标签奖励信号

Result: 优化这种循环一致性结构能够减轻模态特定错误，将推理准确性提升高达7.6个百分点

Conclusion: 高级推理能力的涌现不仅来自数据规模的扩大，还来自对世界结构一致性的强制要求，跨模态不一致性为学习提供了有价值的信号

Abstract: Robust perception and reasoning require consistency across sensory modalities. Yet current multimodal models often violate this principle, yielding contradictory predictions for visual and textual representations of the same concept. Rather than masking these failures with standard voting mechanisms, which can amplify systematic biases, we show that cross-modal inconsistency provides a rich and natural signal for learning. We introduce RC2, a reinforcement learning framework that resolves internal conflicts by enforcing cross-modal cycle consistency. By requiring a model to perform backward inference, switch modalities, and reliably reconstruct the answer through forward inference, we obtain a dense, label-free reward. This cyclic constraint encourages the model to align its internal representations autonomously. Optimizing for this structure mitigates modality-specific errors and improves reasoning accuracy by up to 7.6 points. Our results suggest that advanced reasoning emerges not only from scaling data, but also from enforcing a structurally consistent understanding of the world.

### [201] [Back to Basics: Revisiting ASR in the Age of Voice Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25727)
*Geeyang Tay,Wentao Ma,Jaewon Lee,Yuzhi Tang,Daniel Lee,Weisu Yin,Dongming Shen,Silin Meng,Yi Zhu,Mu Li,Alex Smola*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: WildASR是一个多语言诊断基准，用于评估ASR系统在真实语音条件下的鲁棒性，发现现有系统在环境退化、人口统计偏移和语言多样性方面存在严重且不均衡的性能下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前ASR系统在精心策划的基准测试中已达到接近人类的准确率，但在真实语音助手场景中仍会失败，且现有评估无法系统性地覆盖这些失败条件。缺乏能够隔离特定失败因素的诊断工具，使得从业者无法预测哪些条件、在哪些语言中会导致何种程度的性能下降。

Method: 引入WildASR基准，这是一个完全基于真实人类语音的多语言（四种语言）诊断基准，将ASR鲁棒性沿着三个轴进行分解：环境退化、人口统计偏移和语言多样性。评估了七个广泛使用的ASR系统，并提供了三种分析工具供从业者指导部署决策。

Result: 评估发现ASR系统存在严重且不均衡的性能下降，模型鲁棒性在不同语言和条件之间无法迁移。关键发现是模型在部分或退化的输入下经常产生合理但未说出的内容（幻觉），为下游智能体行为带来具体的安全风险。

Conclusion: 有针对性的、因素隔离的评估对于理解和改进生产系统中ASR的可靠性至关重要。除了基准本身，还提供了三种分析工具，帮助从业者指导部署决策。

Abstract: Automatic speech recognition (ASR) systems have achieved near-human accuracy on curated benchmarks, yet still fail in real-world voice agents under conditions that current evaluations do not systematically cover. Without diagnostic tools that isolate specific failure factors, practitioners cannot anticipate which conditions, in which languages, will cause what degree of degradation. We introduce WildASR, a multilingual (four-language) diagnostic benchmark sourced entirely from real human speech that factorizes ASR robustness along three axes: environmental degradation, demographic shift, and linguistic diversity. Evaluating seven widely used ASR systems, we find severe and uneven performance degradation, and model robustness does not transfer across languages or conditions. Critically, models often hallucinate plausible but unspoken content under partial or degraded inputs, creating concrete safety risks for downstream agent behavior. Our results demonstrate that targeted, factor-isolated evaluation is essential for understanding and improving ASR reliability in production systems. Besides the benchmark itself, we also present three analytical tools that practitioners can use to guide deployment decisions.

</details>

### [202] [Belief-Driven Multi-Agent Collaboration via Approximate Perfect Bayesian Equilibrium for Social Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24973)
*Weiwei Fang,Lin Li,Kaize Shi,Yu Yang,Jianwei Zhang*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: BEACOF是一个基于信念驱动的自适应协作框架，通过建模不完全信息动态博弈来解决现有LLM多智能体框架中静态交互拓扑导致的"群体思维"或僵局问题，实现更真实的社会模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于LLM的多智能体框架主要采用静态交互拓扑，无法捕捉现实世界中合作知识综合与竞争批判性推理之间的动态振荡，导致不现实的"群体思维"或无结果的僵局，影响了社会模拟的可信度。

Method: 提出BEACOF（信念驱动自适应协作框架），受完美贝叶斯均衡启发，将社会互动建模为不完全信息动态博弈，通过迭代精炼对同伴能力的概率信念并自主调整协作策略，解决协作类型选择与能力估计之间的循环依赖问题。

Result: 在对抗性（司法）、开放性（社交）和混合（医疗）场景中验证，BEACOF能够防止协调失败，促进高质量解决方案的稳健收敛，展示了可靠社会模拟的优越潜力。

Conclusion: BEACOF通过动态博弈建模和自适应协作策略，有效解决了现有多智能体框架的局限性，为高保真社会模拟提供了可靠的方法论基础。

Abstract: High-fidelity social simulation is pivotal for addressing complex Web societal challenges, yet it demands agents capable of authentically replicating the dynamic spectrum of human interaction. Current LLM-based multi-agent frameworks, however, predominantly adhere to static interaction topologies, failing to capture the fluid oscillation between cooperative knowledge synthesis and competitive critical reasoning seen in real-world scenarios. This rigidity often leads to unrealistic ``groupthink'' or unproductive deadlocks, undermining the credibility of simulations for decision support. To bridge this gap, we propose \textit{BEACOF}, a \textit{belief-driven adaptive collaboration framework} inspired by Perfect Bayesian Equilibrium (PBE). By modeling social interaction as a dynamic game of incomplete information, BEACOF rigorously addresses the circular dependency between collaboration type selection and capability estimation. Agents iteratively refine probabilistic beliefs about peer capabilities and autonomously modulate their collaboration strategy, thereby ensuring sequentially rational decisions under uncertainty. Validated across adversarial (judicial), open-ended (social) and mixed (medical) scenarios, BEACOF prevents coordination failures and fosters robust convergence toward high-quality solutions, demonstrating superior potential for reliable social simulation. Source codes and datasets are publicly released at: https://github.com/WUT-IDEA/BEACOF.

</details>


### [203] [Ultra-fast Traffic Nowcasting and Control via Differentiable Agent-based Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25068)
*Fumiyasu Makinoshima,Yuya Yamaguchi,Eigo Segawa,Koichiro Niinuma,Sean Qian*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种可微分的基于智能体的交通模拟器，能够实现超快速模型校准、交通实时预测和控制，为交通数字孪生提供实用计算基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统细粒度交通模拟不可微分，依赖低效的无梯度优化，使得实际应用中的模型校准计算不可行。需要一种可微分的方法来实现交通数字孪生的实用化。

Method: 开发了可微分计算技术来模拟单个车辆运动，包括随机决策和智能体间交互，同时确保整个模拟轨迹保持端到端可微分，以便进行高效的基于梯度的优化。

Result: 在芝加哥大规模路网（超过10,000个校准参数）上，模型以173倍实时速度模拟超过100万辆车辆。模型校准仅需455秒，一小时交通预测仅需21秒，交通控制问题解决仅需728秒，整个校准-预测-控制循环在20分钟内完成。

Conclusion: 该工作为交通数字孪生的实现提供了实用的计算基础，能够在40分钟提前时间内实施干预措施，有效解决快速城市化世界中的社会挑战。

Abstract: Traffic digital twins, which inform policymakers of effective interventions based on large-scale, high-fidelity computational models calibrated to real-world traffic, hold promise for addressing societal challenges in our rapidly urbanizing world. However, conventional fine-grained traffic simulations are non-differentiable and typically rely on inefficient gradient-free optimization, making calibration for real-world applications computationally infeasible. Here we present a differentiable agent-based traffic simulator that enables ultra-fast model calibration, traffic nowcasting, and control on large-scale networks. We develop several differentiable computing techniques for simulating individual vehicle movements, including stochastic decision-making and inter-agent interactions, while ensuring that entire simulation trajectories remain end-to-end differentiable for efficient gradient-based optimization. On the large-scale Chicago road network, with over 10,000 calibration parameters, our model simulates more than one million vehicles at 173 times real-time speed. This ultra-fast simulation, together with efficient gradient-based optimization, enables us to complete model calibration using the previous 30 minutes of traffic data in 455 s, provide a one-hour-ahead traffic nowcast in 21 s, and solve the resulting traffic control problem in 728 s. This yields a full calibration--nowcast--control loop in under 20 minutes, leaving about 40 minutes of lead time for implementing interventions. Our work thus provides a practical computational basis for realizing traffic digital twins.

</details>


### [204] [AD-CARE: A Guideline-grounded, Modality-agnostic LLM Agent for Real-world Alzheimer's Disease Diagnosis with Multi-cohort Assessment, Fairness Analysis, and Reader Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25322)
*Wenlong Hou,Sheng Bi,Guangqian Yang,Lihao Liu,Ye Du,Hanxiao Xue,Juncheng Wang,Yuxiang Feng,Yue Xun,Nanxi Yu,Ning Mao,Mo Yang,Yi Wah Eva Cheung,Ling Long,Kay Chen Tan,Lequan Yu,Xiaomeng Ma,Shaozhen Yan,Shujun Wang*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: AD-CARE是一个基于大语言模型的多模态阿尔茨海默病诊断框架，能够从不完整、异质的数据中生成符合临床指南的诊断报告，在多个队列中实现84.9%的诊断准确率，减少亚组间性能差异，并提高临床医生决策效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿尔茨海默病诊断面临现实世界数据不完整、异质性强、跨站点和人口统计学差异大等挑战。现有大语言模型在AD领域主要局限于回答特定问题，而非生成支持临床决策的综合诊断报告。

Method: AD-CARE是一个模态无关的智能体，通过动态编排专业诊断工具并将临床指南嵌入到LLM驱动的推理中，能够从不完整、异质的输入数据中生成透明、报告式的输出，无需对缺失模态进行插补。

Result: 在6个队列共10,303个病例中，AD-CARE达到84.9%诊断准确率，相对基线方法提升4.2%-13.7%。减少种族和年龄亚组间的性能差异（分别降低21%-68%和28%-51%），在读者研究中提高神经科医生和放射科医生准确率6%-11%，并缩短一半决策时间。

Conclusion: AD-CARE是一个可扩展、可实际部署的框架，能够整合到常规临床工作流程中，为阿尔茨海默病的多模态决策提供支持，展示了LLM在临床决策支持中的潜力。

Abstract: Alzheimer's disease (AD) is a growing global health challenge as populations age, and timely, accurate diagnosis is essential to reduce individual and societal burden. However, real-world AD assessment is hampered by incomplete, heterogeneous multimodal data and variability across sites and patient demographics. Although large language models (LLMs) have shown promise in biomedicine, their use in AD has largely been confined to answering narrow, disease-specific questions rather than generating comprehensive diagnostic reports that support clinical decision-making. Here we expand LLM capabilities for clinical decision support by introducing AD-CARE, a modality-agnostic agent that performs guideline-grounded diagnostic assessment from incomplete, heterogeneous inputs without imputing missing modalities. By dynamically orchestrating specialized diagnostic tools and embedding clinical guidelines into LLM-driven reasoning, AD-CARE generates transparent, report-style outputs aligned with real-world clinical workflows. Across six cohorts comprising 10,303 cases, AD-CARE achieved 84.9% diagnostic accuracy, delivering 4.2%-13.7% relative improvements over baseline methods. Despite cohort-level differences, dataset-specific accuracies remain robust (80.4%-98.8%), and the agent consistently outperforms all baselines. AD-CARE reduced performance disparities across racial and age subgroups, decreasing the average dispersion of four metrics by 21%-68% and 28%-51%, respectively. In a controlled reader study, the agent improved neurologist and radiologist accuracy by 6%-11% and more than halved decision time. The framework yielded 2.29%-10.66% absolute gains over eight backbone LLMs and converges their performance. These results show that AD-CARE is a scalable, practically deployable framework that can be integrated into routine clinical workflows for multimodal decision support in AD.

</details>

### [205] [SolRugDetector: Investigating Rug Pulls on Solana](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24625)
*Jiaxin Chen,Ziwei Li,Zigui Jiang,Ruihong He,Yantong Zhou,Jiajing Wu,Zibin Zheng*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 该论文对Solana区块链上的Rug Pull欺诈行为进行了首次系统性实证研究，构建了标注数据集，开发了检测系统SolRugDetector，并在大规模测量中识别了大量欺诈代币，揭示了Solana上Rug Pull的独特特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Solana因其高性能和低交易成本而快速增长，但极低的代币发行门槛导致了广泛的Rug Pull欺诈。与依赖恶意智能合约的以太坊Rug Pull不同，Solana上的统一SPL代币程序将欺诈行为转向链上操作（如市场操纵），现有研究尚未对这些特定模式进行系统分析。

Method: 基于68个真实事件报告构建了包含117个确认Rug Pull代币的手动标注数据集，并提出了SolRugDetector检测系统，该系统仅使用链上交易和状态数据识别欺诈代币。随后对2025年上半年新发行的100,063个代币进行了大规模测量。

Result: 实验结果显示SolRugDetector在标注数据集上优于现有工具。大规模测量识别出76,469个Rug Pull代币。分析发现Solana上的Rug Pull具有极短的生命周期、强烈的价格驱动动态、严重的经济损失和高度组织化的群体行为。

Conclusion: 该研究首次系统分析了Solana上的Rug Pull模式，揭示了其独特特征，为理解Solana欺诈生态提供了重要见解，并支持开发有效的链上防御机制。研究发布的数据集和检测工具对社区具有重要价值。

Abstract: Solana has experienced rapid growth due to its high performance and low transaction costs, but the extremely low barrier to token issuance has also led to widespread Rug Pulls. Unlike Ethereum-based Rug Pulls that rely on malicious smart contracts, the unified SPL Token program on Solana shifts fraudulent behaviors toward on-chain operations such as market manipulation. However, existing research has not yet conducted a systematic analysis of these specific Rug Pull patterns on Solana. In this paper, we present a comprehensive empirical study of Rug Pulls on Solana. Based on 68 real-world incident reports, we construct and release a manually labeled dataset containing 117 confirmed Rug Pull tokens and characterize the workflow of Rug Pulls on Solana. Building on this analysis, we propose SolRugDetector, a detection system that identifies fraudulent tokens solely using on-chain transaction and state data. Experimental results show that SolRugDetector outperforms existing tools on the labeled dataset. We further conduct a large-scale measurement on 100,063 tokens newly issued in the first half of 2025 and identify 76,469 Rug Pull tokens. After validating the in-the-wild detection results, we release this dataset and analyze the Rug Pull ecosystem on Solana. Our analysis reveals that Rug Pulls on Solana exhibit extremely short lifecycles, strong price-driven dynamics, severe economic losses, and highly organized group behaviors. These findings provide insights into the Solana Rug Pull landscape and support the development of effective on-chain defense mechanisms.

</details>


### [206] [Bridging Code Property Graphs and Language Models for Program Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24837)
*Ahmed Lekssays*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: CodeBadger是一个开源MCP服务器，将Joern的代码属性图引擎与LLM集成，通过高级工具实现跨函数和文件的代码分析，解决LLM在安全漏洞分析中的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在分析真实世界代码库中的安全漏洞时面临关键挑战：token限制无法加载整个仓库，代码嵌入无法捕获过程间数据流，LLM难以生成复杂的静态分析查询。现有方法只能处理孤立的代码片段，无法发现跨多个函数和文件的漏洞。

Method: 引入CodeBadger开源MCP服务器，集成Joern的代码属性图引擎与LLM。提供程序切片、污点跟踪、数据流分析和语义代码导航等高级工具，无需LLM生成复杂的CPG查询，实现对大型代码库的针对性探索。

Result: 通过三个用例展示有效性：(1)在8000个方法的代码库中审计内存安全模式；(2)发现并利用libtiff中先前未报告的缓冲区溢出漏洞；(3)首次尝试即为libxml2中的整数溢出漏洞(CVE-2025-6021)生成正确补丁。

Conclusion: CodeBadger使LLM能够在整个仓库范围内进行语义代码推理，支持大规模漏洞发现、补丁生成和程序理解。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) face critical challenges when analyzing security vulnerabilities in real world codebases: token limits prevent loading entire repositories, code embeddings fail to capture inter procedural data flows, and LLMs struggle to generate complex static analysis queries. These limitations force existing approaches to operate on isolated code snippets, missing vulnerabilities that span multiple functions and files. We introduce codebadger, an open source Model Context Protocol (MCP) server that integrates Joern's Code Property Graph (CPG) engine with LLMs. Rather than requiring LLMs to generate complex CPG queries, codebadger provides high level tools for program slicing, taint tracking, data flow analysis, and semantic code navigation, enabling targeted exploration of large codebases without exhaustive file reading. We demonstrate its effectiveness through three use cases: (1) navigating an 8,000 method codebase to audit memory safety patterns, (2) discovering and exploiting a previously unreported buffer overflow in libtiff, and (3) generating a correct patch for an integer overflow vulnerability (CVE-2025-6021) in libxml2 on the first attempt. codebadger enables LLMs to reason about code semantically across entire repositories, supporting vulnerability discovery, patching, and program comprehension at scale.

</details>


### [207] [AI Security in the Foundation Model Era: A Comprehensive Survey from a Unified Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24857)
*Zhenyi Wang,Siyu Luan*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个统一闭环威胁分类法，将机器学习安全威胁按照数据与模型之间的双向交互关系分为四类，以解决现有研究中威胁分析碎片化的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着机器学习系统规模和功能的扩展，安全威胁日益复杂，但现有研究往往孤立地看待这些威胁，缺乏一个统一的框架来揭示它们之间的共同原理和相互依赖关系。这种碎片化的视角阻碍了对机器学习安全的系统性理解，也限制了全面防御的设计。特别是，机器学习的两大基础资产——数据和模型——不再独立，一方的漏洞会直接影响另一方。

Method: 提出了一个统一闭环威胁分类法，该框架沿着四个方向轴明确地构建了模型与数据之间的交互关系：数据→数据、数据→模型、模型→数据、模型→模型。

Result: 该框架将机器学习安全威胁分为四类：(1) 数据→数据：包括数据解密攻击和水印移除攻击；(2) 数据→模型：包括投毒攻击、有害微调攻击和越狱攻击；(3) 模型→数据：包括模型反演、成员推理攻击和训练数据提取攻击；(4) 模型→模型：包括模型提取攻击。

Conclusion: 这个统一框架阐明了这些安全威胁之间的内在联系，为开发可扩展、可迁移和跨模态的安全策略奠定了基础，特别是在基础模型的背景下。

Abstract: As machine learning (ML) systems expand in both scale and functionality, the security landscape has become increasingly complex, with a proliferation of attacks and defenses. However, existing studies largely treat these threats in isolation, lacking a coherent framework to expose their shared principles and interdependencies. This fragmented view hinders systematic understanding and limits the design of comprehensive defenses. Crucially, the two foundational assets of ML -- \textbf{data} and \textbf{models} -- are no longer independent; vulnerabilities in one directly compromise the other. The absence of a holistic framework leaves open questions about how these bidirectional risks propagate across the ML pipeline. To address this critical gap, we propose a \emph{unified closed-loop threat taxonomy} that explicitly frames model-data interactions along four directional axes. Our framework offers a principled lens for analyzing and defending foundation models. The resulting four classes of security threats represent distinct but interrelated categories of attacks: (1) Data$\rightarrow$Data (D$\rightarrow$D): including \emph{data decryption attacks and watermark removal attacks}; (2) Data$\rightarrow$Model (D$\rightarrow$M): including \emph{poisoning, harmful fine-tuning attacks, and jailbreak attacks}; (3) Model$\rightarrow$Data (M$\rightarrow$D): including \emph{model inversion, membership inference attacks, and training data extraction attacks}; (4) Model$\rightarrow$Model (M$\rightarrow$M): including \emph{model extraction attacks}. Our unified framework elucidates the underlying connections among these security threats and establishes a foundation for developing scalable, transferable, and cross-modal security strategies, particularly within the landscape of foundation models.

</details>


### [208] [Trusted-Execution Environment (TEE) for Solving the Replication Crisis in Academia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24878)
*Jiasun Li,Project Team*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出基于可信执行环境(TEE)的新框架，通过云端TEE执行复制包并提交加密执行证明，以低成本、可扩展方式解决学术研究的可重复性危机。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经济学、金融学、社会科学和计算机科学等领域日益严重的可重复性危机正在削弱学术研究的可信度。现有的制度解决方案（如工件评估和复制包）存在关键局限性：合格数据编辑人员短缺、处理专有数据集困难、流程效率低下以及依赖志愿劳动。

Method: 提出一个利用可信执行环境（TEE）技术（如Intel TDX）的新框架。作者在云端TEE中执行复制包，并提交正确执行的加密证明，期刊或会议无需重新运行代码即可高效验证。这种方法将操作负担转移给作者，同时保护数据机密性并减少对稀缺编辑资源的依赖。

Result: 通过实地实验验证了系统的可行性，在TDX支持的云端虚拟机上进行试点研究，平均成本为每包1.35-1.80美元，相对于标准虚拟机计算开销最小，即使是没有TEE经验的新手用户也能获得高成功率。形式分析表明TEE采用对作者具有激励兼容性，对期刊具有成本优势，并在认证市场中构成均衡。

Conclusion: TEE技术有潜力为学术界的可重复性危机提供可持续、隐私保护和高效的解决方案，能够以成本效益高且可扩展的方式解决当前制度方案的局限性。

Abstract: The growing replication crisis across disciplines such as economics, finance, and other social sciences as well as computer science undermines the credibility of academic research. Current institutional solutions -- such as artifact evaluations and replication packages -- suffer from critical limitations, including shortages of qualified data editors, difficulties in handling proprietary datasets, inefficient processes, and reliance on voluntary labor. This paper proposes a novel framework leveraging new technological advances in trusted-execution environments (TEEs) -- exemplified by Intel Trust Domain Extensions (TDX) -- to address the replication crisis in a cost-effective and scalable manner. Under our approach, authors execute replication packages within a cloud-based TEE and submit cryptographic proofs of correct execution, for which journals or conferences can efficiently verify without re-running the code. This reallocates the operational burden to authors while preserving data confidentiality and eliminating reliance on scarce editorial resources. As a proof of concept, we validate the feasibility of this system through field experiments, reporting a pilot study replicating published papers on TDX-backed cloud VMs, finding average costs of \$1.35--\$1.80 per package with minimal computational overhead relative to standard VMs and high success rates even for novice users with no prior TEE experience. We also provide a conduct formal analysis showing that TEE adoption is incentive-compatible for authors, cost-dominant for journals, and constitutes an equilibrium in the certification market. The findings highlight the potential of TEE technology to provide a sustainable, privacy-preserving, and efficient mechanism to address the replication crisis in academia.

</details>


### [209] [LiteGuard: Efficient Task-Agnostic Model Fingerprinting with Enhanced Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24982)
*Guang Yang,Ziye Geng,Yihang Chen,Changqing Luo*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: LiteGuard：一种高效的任务无关模型指纹框架，通过检查点模型增强和本地验证器设计，在减少计算成本的同时提升泛化性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前最先进的MetaV方法需要大量不同模型进行训练，但现实世界中公开可用模型稀缺，构建这样的模型集需要大量计算资源。减少模型数量会导致过拟合问题，MetaV的纠缠设计进一步加剧了这个问题，影响了验证未见模型的泛化能力。

Method: LiteGuard提出两个关键创新：1）检查点模型增强策略，利用每个盗版模型和独立训练模型训练过程中的中间快照来丰富模型多样性；2）本地验证器架构，为每个指纹配备轻量级本地验证器，减少参数纠缠并缓解过拟合。

Result: 在五个代表性任务上的广泛实验表明，LiteGuard在泛化性能和计算效率方面始终优于MetaV。

Conclusion: LiteGuard提供了一种高效的任务无关指纹框架，能够在显著降低计算成本的同时实现更好的泛化能力，解决了现有方法在实际部署中的资源限制和过拟合问题。

Abstract: Task-agnostic model fingerprinting has recently gained increasing attention due to its ability to provide a universal framework applicable across diverse model architectures and tasks. The current state-of-the-art method, MetaV, ensures generalization by jointly training a set of fingerprints and a neural-network-based global verifier using two large and diverse model sets: one composed of pirated models (i.e., the protected model and its variants) and the other comprising independently trained models. However, publicly available models are scarce in many real-world domains, and constructing such model sets requires intensive training and massive computational resources, posing a significant barrier to deployment. Reducing the number of models can alleviate the overhead, but increases the risk of overfitting, a problem further exacerbated by MetaV's entangled design, in which all fingerprints and the global verifier are jointly trained. This overfitting issue compromises the generalization capability for verifying unseen models.
  In this paper, we propose LiteGuard, an efficient task-agnostic fingerprinting framework that attains enhanced generalization while significantly lowering computational cost. Specifically, LiteGuard introduces two key innovations: (i) a checkpoint-based model set augmentation strategy that enriches model diversity by leveraging intermediate model snapshots captured during training of each pirated and independently trained model, thereby alleviating the need to train a large number of such models, and (ii) a local verifier architecture that pairs each fingerprint with a lightweight local verifier, thereby reducing parameter entanglement and mitigating overfitting. Extensive experiments across five representative tasks show that LiteGuard consistently outperforms MetaV in both generalization performance and computational efficiency.

</details>


### [210] [IrisFP: Adversarial-Example-based Model Fingerprinting with Enhanced Uniqueness and Robustness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24996)
*Ziye Geng,Guang Yang,Yihang Chen,Changqing Luo*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: IrisFP是一种基于对抗样本的模型指纹框架，通过利用多边界特性、多样本行为和指纹判别力评估来生成复合样本指纹，显著提高了唯一性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型指纹方法通常针对单一决策边界，导致指纹的唯一性和鲁棒性不足。需要开发一种能够同时增强这两方面性能的新方法，以可靠地验证模型所有权。

Method: 1) 将指纹定位在所有决策边界的交点附近，而不是单一边界；2) 构建复合样本指纹，每个指纹包含多个靠近多边界交点的样本；3) 使用基于两个参考模型集（盗版模型和独立训练模型）开发的统计可分性指标评估指纹的判别力，保留高判别力指纹并分配特定阈值。

Result: 大量实验表明，IrisFP在唯一性和鲁棒性方面一致优于现有最先进方法，实现了可靠的模型所有权验证。

Conclusion: IrisFP通过创新的多边界定位、复合样本构建和判别力评估机制，成功解决了模型指纹的唯一性和鲁棒性平衡问题，为可靠的模型所有权验证提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: We propose IrisFP, a novel adversarial-example-based model fingerprinting framework that enhances both uniqueness and robustness by leveraging multi-boundary characteristics, multi-sample behaviors, and fingerprint discriminative power assessment to generate composite-sample fingerprints. Three key innovations make IrisFP outstanding: 1) It positions fingerprints near the intersection of all decision boundaries - unlike prior methods that target a single boundary - thus increasing the prediction margin without placing fingerprints deep inside target class regions, enhancing both robustness and uniqueness; 2) It constructs composite-sample fingerprints, each comprising multiple samples close to the multi-boundary intersection, to exploit collective behavior patterns and further boost uniqueness; and 3) It assesses the discriminative power of generated fingerprints using statistical separability metrics developed based on two reference model sets, respectively, for pirated and independently-trained models, retains the fingerprints with high discriminative power, and assigns fingerprint-specific thresholds to such retained fingerprints. Extensive experiments show that IrisFP consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods, achieving reliable ownership verification by enhancing both robustness and uniqueness.

</details>


### [211] [Efficient ML-DSA Public Key Management Method with Identity for PKI and Its Application](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25043)
*Penghui Liu,Yi Niu,Xiaoxiong Zhong,Jiahui Wu,Weizhe Zhang,Kaiping Xue,Bin Xiao*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于后量子密码的身份公钥管理框架IPK-pq，用于解决传统PKI在工业物联网大规模场景下的证书存储、验证和传输问题，并在RPKI系统中验证了其效率和可扩展性优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着工业物联网的快速发展，传统基于证书的PKI在大规模证书存储、验证和频繁传输场景中的局限性日益明显，后量子密码的广泛应用将进一步加剧这些挑战。

Method: 提出IPK-pq身份公钥管理框架，基于NIST ML-DSA和随机矩阵理论实现身份密钥生成协议，通过增强的身份映射机制解决CPK的线性共谋问题，简化公钥真实性验证。

Result: 为IPK-pq提供了形式化安全证明，涵盖单个私钥组件和复合私钥；在RPKI典型应用场景中实现并评估，实验结果表明基于IPK-pq的RPKI系统在效率和可扩展性方面有显著提升。

Conclusion: IPK-pq验证了其可行性和合理性，可作为下一代RPKI系统的有力候选方案，能够安全地管理大规模路由信息。

Abstract: With the rapid evolution of the Industrial Internet of Things (IIoT), the boundaries and scale of the Internet are continuously expanding. Consequently, the limitations of traditional certificate-based Public Key Infrastructure (PKI) have become increasingly evident, particularly in scenarios requiring large-scale certificate storage, verification, and frequent transmission. These challenges are expected to be further amplified by the widespread adoption of post-quantum cryptography. In this paper, we propose a novel identity-based public key management framework for PKI based on post-quantum cryptography, termed \textit{IPK-pq}. This approach implements an identity key generation protocol leveraging NIST ML-DSA and random matrix theory. Building on the concept of the Composite Public Key (CPK), \textit{IPK-pq} addresses the linear collusion problem inherent in CPK through an enhanced identity mapping mechanism. Furthermore, it simplifies the verification of the declared public key's authenticity, effectively reducing the complexity associated with certificate-based key management. We also provide a formal security proof for \textit{IPK-pq}, covering both individual private key components and the composite private key. To validate our approach, formally, we directly implement and evaluate \textit{IPK-pq} within a typical PKI application scenario: Resource PKI (RPKI). Comparative experimental results demonstrate that an RPKI system based on \textit{IPK-pq} yields significant improvements in efficiency and scalability. These results validate the feasibility and rationality of \textit{IPK-pq}, positioning it as a strong candidate for next-generation RPKI systems capable of securely managing large-scale routing information.

### [212] [PIDP-Attack: Combining Prompt Injection with Database Poisoning Attacks on Retrieval-Augmented Generation Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25164)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管RAG系统通过外部知识源增强了LLM，但仍面临对抗攻击威胁。现有投毒攻击需要预先知道用户具体查询，限制了灵活性和实际应用性。

Method: 提出PIDP-Attack复合攻击方法：1) 在推理时向查询附加恶意字符（提示注入）；2) 向检索数据库注入少量投毒段落；3) 结合两种攻击无需预先知道用户实际查询即可操控LLM响应。

Result: 在三个基准数据集（Natural Questions、HotpotQA、MS-MARCO）和八个LLM上的实验表明，PIDP-Attack始终优于原始PoisonedRAG，在开放域QA任务上攻击成功率提升4%-16%，同时保持高检索精度。

Conclusion: 复合攻击策略既必要又高效，PIDP-Attack通过结合提示注入和数据库投毒，显著提升了RAG系统的攻击成功率，无需预先知道用户查询，具有更强的实际应用性。

However, their practical deployment is often hindered by issues such as outdated knowledge and the tendency to generate hallucinations. To address these limitations, Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems have been introduced, enhancing LLMs with external, up-to-date knowledge sources. Despite their advantages, RAG systems remain vulnerable to adversarial attacks, with data poisoning emerging as a prominent threat. Existing poisoning-based attacks typically require prior knowledge of the user's specific queries, limiting their flexibility and real-world applicability. In this work, we propose PIDP-Attack, a novel compound attack that integrates prompt injection with database poisoning in RAG. By appending malicious characters to queries at inference time and injecting a limited number of poisoned passages into the retrieval database, our method can effectively manipulate LLM response to arbitrary query without prior knowledge of the user's actual query. Experimental evaluations across three benchmark datasets (Natural Questions, HotpotQA, MS-MARCO) and eight LLMs demonstrate that PIDP-Attack consistently outperforms the original PoisonedRAG. Specifically, our method improves attack success rates by 4% to 16% on open-domain QA tasks while maintaining high retrieval precision, proving that the compound attack strategy is both necessary and highly effective.

### [214] [Physical Backdoor Attack Against Deep Learning-Based Modulation Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25304)
*Younes Salmi,Hanna Bogucka*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出使用功率放大器非线性失真作为物理触发器，在数据集形成前创建物理触发。训练阶段，攻击者操纵RF信号幅度并将其标签更改为目标调制方案，训练出后门模型。推理阶段，攻击者保持后门不活跃以维持高测试精度，但应用与训练阶段相同的操纵即可激活后门导致误分类。

Result: 实验表明，所提出的攻击方法在不同噪声水平下仅需少量操纵的RF信号即可实现高攻击成功率。此外，测试了多种防御技术对该攻击的抵御能力，结果显示这些防御技术均无法有效缓解该攻击。

Conclusion: 本文成功演示了一种针对DL调制分类器的物理后门攻击，该攻击利用功率放大器非线性失真作为物理触发器，具有高攻击成功率和强隐蔽性，现有防御技术难以检测和缓解，揭示了物理层安全威胁的重要性。

Abstract: Deep Learning (DL) has become a key technology that assists radio frequency (RF) signal classification applications, such as modulation classification. However, the DL models are vulnerable to adversarial machine learning threats, such as data manipulation attacks. We study a physical backdoor (Trojan) attack that targets a DL-based modulation classifier. In contrast to digital backdoor attacks, where digital triggers are injected into the training dataset, we use power amplifier (PA) non-linear distortions to create physical triggers before the dataset is formed. During training, the adversary manipulates amplitudes of RF signals and changes their labels to a target modulation scheme, training a backdoored model. At inference, the adversary aims to keep the backdoor attack inactive such that the backdoored model maintains high accuracy on test signals. However, if they apply the same manipulation used during training on these test signals, the backdoor is activated, and the model misclassifies these signals. We demonstrate that our proposed attack achieves high attack success rates with few manipulated RD signals for different noise levels. Furthermore, we test the resilience of the proposed attack to multiple defense techniques, and the results show that these techniques fail to mitigate the attack.

Among these approaches, Coverage-based grey-box fuzzing, which utilizes runtime code coverage information, has become the dominant methodology. Conventional fuzzing techniques primarily target a single software component and have paid little attention to cooperative execution with other software. In this study, we investigate fuzzing techniques for architectures in which an operating system and firmware operate cooperatively. However, we show that the architectural shift toward Dynamic High-Resolution preprocessing (e.g., AnyRes) introduces an inherent algorithmic side-channel. Unlike static models, dynamic preprocessing decomposes images into a variable number of patches based on their aspect ratio, creating workload-dependent inputs. We demonstrate a dual-layer attack framework against local VLMs. In Tier 1, an unprivileged attacker can exploit significant execution-time variations using standard unprivileged OS metrics to reliably fingerprint the input's geometry. In Tier 2, by profiling Last-Level Cache (LLC) contention, the attacker can resolve semantic ambiguity within identical geometries, distinguishing between visually dense (e.g., medical X-rays) and sparse (e.g., text documents) content. By evaluating state-of-the-art models such as LLaVA-NeXT and Qwen2-VL, we show that combining these signals enables reliable inference of privacy-sensitive contexts. Finally, we analyze the security engineering trade-offs of mitigating this vulnerability, reveal substantial performance overhead with constant-work padding, and propose practical design recommendations for secure Edge AI deployments.

Method: 基于对抗损失子空间分解，提出TAAC框架，包含区分特征子空间分解器、灵活噪声加密器和分阶段训练范式

Result: 实验证明该框架在抑郁症检测、身份信息保留和音频重建方面优于现有加密方法，在不同加密强度下保持稳定

Conclusion: TAAC框架在保密性、准确性、可追溯性和可调节性方面表现优异，为可信音频情感计算提供实用解决方案

Abstract: With the emergence of AI techniques for depression diagnosis, the conflict between high demand and limited supply for depression screening has been significantly alleviated. Among various modal data, audio-based depression diagnosis has received increasing attention from both academia and industry since audio is the most common carrier of emotion transmission. Unfortunately, audio data also contains User-sensitive Identity Information (ID), which is extremely vulnerable and may be maliciously used during the smart diagnosis process. Among previous methods, the clarification between depression features and sensitive features has always serve as a barrier. It is also critical to the problem for introducing a safe encryption methodology that only encrypts the sensitive features and a powerful classifier that can correctly diagnose the depression. To track these challenges, by leveraging adversarial loss-based Subspace Decomposition, we propose a first practical framework \name presented for Trustable Audio Affective Computing, to perform automated depression detection through audio within a trustable environment. The key enablers of TAAC are Differentiating Features Subspace Decompositor (DFSD), Flexible Noise Encryptor (FNE) and Staged Training Paradigm, used for decomposition, ID encryption and performance enhancement, respectively. Extensive experiments with existing encryption methods demonstrate our framework's preeminent performance in depression detection, ID reservation and audio reconstruction. Meanwhile, the experiments across various setting demonstrates our model's stability under different encryption strengths. Thus proving our framework's excellence in Confidentiality, Accuracy, Traceability, and Adjustability.

</details>

### [221] [Sketch2Simulation: Automating Flowsheet Generation via Multi Agent Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24629)
*Abdullah Bahamdan,Emma Pajak,John D. Hedengren,Antonio del Rio Chanona*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 开发了一个端到端多智能体LLM系统，将工艺流程图直接转换为可执行的Aspen HYSYS流程模拟文件，实现了从草图到模拟的自动化工作流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将工艺草图转换为可执行模拟模型是过程系统工程中的主要瓶颈，需要大量手动工作和模拟器专业知识。现有的生成式AI方法在工程图理解和LLM辅助流程生成方面虽有进展，但两者脱节：图理解方法通常只提取图形，而文本到模拟工作流假设结构化输入而非原始视觉数据。

Method: 提出了一个端到端多智能体大语言模型系统，将任务分解为三个协调层：1) 图表解析和解释，2) 模拟模型合成，3) 多层次验证。专用智能体处理视觉解释、基于图的中间表示构建、HYSYS COM接口代码生成、执行和结构验证。

Result: 在四个复杂性递增的化学工程案例研究中评估了该框架：从简单的脱盐过程到具有多个循环回路的工业芳烃生产流程。系统在所有情况下都生成了可执行的HYSYS模型，在两个较简单案例中实现了完全结构保真度，在更复杂案例中表现良好，连接一致性超过0.93，流股一致性超过0.96。

Conclusion: 研究展示了一个可行的端到端草图到模拟工作流，同时突出了在密集循环结构、隐式图语义和模拟器接口约束方面仍存在的挑战。

Abstract: Converting process sketches into executable simulation models remains a major bottleneck in process systems engineering, requiring substantial manual effort and simulator-specific expertise. Recent advances in generative AI have improved both engineering-diagram interpretation and LLM-assisted flowsheet generation, but these remain largely disconnected: diagram-understanding methods often stop at extracted graphs, while text-to-simulation workflows assume structured inputs rather than raw visual artifacts. To bridge this gap, we present an end-to-end multi-agent large language model system that converts process diagrams directly into executable Aspen HYSYS flowsheets. The framework decomposes the task into three coordinated layers: diagram parsing and interpretation, simulation model synthesis, and multi-level validation. Specialized agents handle visual interpretation, graph-based intermediate representation construction, code generation for the HYSYS COM interface, execution, and structural verification. We evaluate the framework on four chemical engineering case studies of increasing complexity, from a simple desalting process to an industrial aromatic production flowsheet with multiple recycle loops. The system produces executable HYSYS models in all cases, achieving complete structural fidelity on the two simpler cases and strong performance on the more complex ones, with connection consistency above 0.93 and stream consistency above 0.96. These results demonstrate a viable end-to-end sketch-to-simulation workflow while highlighting remaining challenges in dense recycle structures, implicit diagram semantics, and simulator-interface constraints.

</details>


### [222] [IndustriConnect: MCP Adapters and Mock-First Evaluation for AI-Assisted Industrial Operations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24703)
*Melwin Xavier,Melveena Jolly,Vaisakh M A,Midhun Xavier*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: INDUSTRICONNECT是一套MCP适配器原型，让AI助手能够通过工业协议（Modbus、MQTT/Sparkplug B、OPC UA）与工业设备交互，提供协议特定的连接和安全控制，并通过本地模拟和确定性基准测试验证其正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI助手能够分解多步骤工作流，但无法原生支持工业协议（如Modbus、MQTT/Sparkplug B、OPC UA），因此需要开发适配器来让AI助手能够与工业设备交互，同时保持协议特定的连接性和安全控制。

Method: 开发INDUSTRICONNECT原型套件，包含MCP适配器，将工业操作暴露为可模式发现的AI工具；采用通用响应信封和模拟优先工作流，允许在连接实际设备前本地测试适配器行为；设计确定性基准测试，涵盖正常、故障注入、压力和恢复场景。

Result: 进行了870次测试运行（480次正常、210次故障注入、120次压力、60次恢复试验），涉及2820次工具调用、7种故障场景和12种压力场景。正常套件完全成功，故障套件确认了结构化错误处理（包括适配器级uint16范围验证），压力套件识别了并发边界，所有三种协议都演示了端点重启后的同会话恢复。

Conclusion: INDUSTRICONNECT为AI辅助的工业操作提供了适配器正确性、并发行为和结构化错误处理的证据，证明了MCP适配器能够有效桥接AI助手与工业协议，同时保持必要的安全控制和协议特性。

Abstract: AI assistants can decompose multi-step workflows, but they do not natively speak industrial protocols such as Modbus, MQTT/Sparkplug B, or OPC UA, so this paper presents INDUSTRICONNECT, a prototype suite of Model Context Protocol (MCP) adapters that expose industrial operations as schema-discoverable AI tools while preserving protocol-specific connectivity and safety controls; the system uses a common response envelope and a mock-first workflow so adapter behavior can be exercised locally before connecting to plant equipment, and a deterministic benchmark covering normal, fault-injected, stress, and recovery scenarios evaluates the flagship adapters, comprising 870 runs (480 normal, 210 fault-injected, 120 stress, 60 recovery trials) and 2820 tool calls across 7 fault scenarios and 12 stress scenarios, where the normal suite achieved full success, the fault suite confirmed structured error handling with adapter-level uint16 range validation, the stress suite identified concurrency boundaries, and same-session recovery after endpoint restart is demonstrated for all three protocols, with results providing evidence spanning adapter correctness, concurrency behavior, and structured error handling for AI-assisted industrial operations.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 该方法允许组织在保留敏捷灵活性的同时，通过里程碑计划确保项目执行与战略目标一致，同时组织可以选择最适合自己的开发方法。

Abstract: Milestone Driven Agile Execution is a hybrid management framework where the empirical control component of agile development is retained but the prioritization of the backlog is done according to a macro or strategic (milestone) plan that drives the execution of the project.
  MDAX is method agnostic, in the sense that the development approach is not embedded in the execution mechanism but in the plan that drives it. This allows organizations using it to choose the development approach that suites them most,

### [225] [Learning From Developers: Towards Reliable Patch Validation at Scale for Linux](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24825)
*Chih-En Lin,Attreyee Mukherjee,Ajay Rawat,Ruqi Zhang,Pedro Fonseca*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: FLINT是一个基于规则和LLM的补丁验证系统框架，通过分析历史开发者讨论来自动验证Linux补丁提案，提高审查效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Linux内存管理子系统补丁审查过程主要依赖人工，随着提交量增加，开发者难以跟上审查需求，且严重依赖少数核心开发者。现有自动化工具覆盖有限，需要更智能的审查辅助系统。

Method: FLINT采用多阶段方法：1) 从历史开发者讨论中提取验证规则；2) 使用无需训练或微调的LLM；3) 当有新补丁提案时，检索相关验证规则进行分析；4) 生成有参考依据的报告供开发者验证。系统针对传统工具难以检测的维护性问题和复杂并发问题。

Result: FLINT在Linux v6.18开发周期中检测到2个新问题，在先前版本中检测到7个问题。在并发bug检测方面，FLINT比仅使用LLM的基线提高了21%和14%的覆盖率。系统假阳性率为35%，低于基线。

Conclusion: FLINT能够有效扩展补丁审查过程，通过利用历史讨论知识自动验证补丁提案，减轻开发者负担，特别在检测传统工具难以发现的复杂问题方面表现出色。

Abstract: Patch reviewing is critical for software development, especially in distributed open-source development, which highly depends on voluntary work, such as Linux. This paper studies the past 10 years of patch reviews of the Linux memory management subsystem to characterize the challenges involved in patch reviewing at scale. Our study reveals that the review process is still primarily reliant on human effort despite a wide-range of automatic checking tools. Although kernel developers strive to review all patch proposals, they struggle to keep up with the increasing volume of submissions and depend significantly on a few developers for these reviews.
  To help scale the patch review process, we introduce FLINT, a patch validation system framework that synthesizes insights from past discussions among developers and automatically analyzes patch proposals for compliance. FLINT employs a rule-based analysis informed by past discussions among developers and an LLM that does not require training or fine-tuning on new data, and can continuously improve with minimum human effort. FLINT uses a multi-stage approach to efficiently distill the essential information from past discussions. Later, when a patch proposal needs review, FLINT retrieves the relevant validation rules for validation and generates a reference-backed report that developers can easily interpret and validate. FLINT targets bugs that traditional tools find hard to detect, ranging from maintainability issues, e.g., design choices and naming conventions, to complex concurrency issues, e.g., deadlocks and data races. FLINT detected 2 new issues in Linux v6.18 development cycle and 7 issues in previous versions. FLINT achieves 21% and 14% of higher ground-truth coverage on concurrency bugs than the baseline with LLM only. Moreover, FLINT achieves a 35% false positive rate, which is lower than the baseline.

</details>


### [226] [Data-Oriented Modeling for Spacecraft Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24841)
*Nathan Strange*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种基于数据导向的MBSE方法，采用游戏行业的实体-组件-系统架构，将设计数据存储为不可变组件，通过无状态分析函数处理数据，以降低航天器开发复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管发射成本下降，但航天器开发成本仍然很高，部分原因是传统MBSE工具继承了面向对象编程范式的复杂性：紧密耦合的数据和逻辑、可变状态、以及难以与专业分析工具集成的刚性类层次结构。

Method: 采用视频游戏行业的实体-组件-系统架构，将设计数据存储为不可变、格式无关的组件；通过模板和容器化工具在持续集成管道中使用无状态分析函数处理这些数据。

Result: 原型实现VVERDAD在一个示例星际任务概念上展示了该方法，表明数据导向原则能够降低部署复杂度、简化测试，并保留基于文档的系统工程的追溯性优势。

Conclusion: 数据导向的MBSE方法通过采用ECS架构，能够有效解决传统MBSE工具的复杂性，提高航天器系统工程的效率和集成能力。

Abstract: Spacecraft development costs remain high despite falling launch costs, in part because Model-Based Systems Engineering (MBSE) tools carry the complexity of the object-oriented programming paradigm: tightly coupled data and logic, mutable state, and rigid class hierarchies that resist integration with discipline-specific analysis tools. This paper presents a data-oriented approach to MBSE that adapts the Entity-Component-System (ECS) architecture from the video game industry. Design data is stored as immutable, format-agnostic components in a generic data system; stateless analysis functions operate on this data through templates and containerized tools within a continuous integration pipeline. A prototype implementation, VVERDAD (https://github.com/VisVivaSpace/vverdad-prototype), demonstrates the approach on an example interplanetary mission concept, showing how data-oriented principles can reduce deployment complexity, simplify testing, and preserve the traceability benefits of document-based systems engineering.

</details>


### [227] [Governance in Practice: How Open Source Projects Define and Document Roles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24879)
*Pedro Oliveira,Tayana Conte,Marco Gerosa,Igor Steinmacher*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究开源软件治理结构，通过分析GOVERNANCE.md文件，发现相同角色名称在不同项目中职责差异很大，存在角色漂移现象，少数核心成员承担过多职责形成治理瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开源软件的可持续性不仅依赖于代码贡献，还取决于治理结构。目前缺乏关于项目如何通过书面文档正式定义角色和权限的系统性实证证据，需要研究开源项目如何通过治理文档构建制度基础设施。

Method: 使用制度语法分析GitHub仓库中的GOVERNANCE.md及相关文档，将每个角色分解为范围、权限、义务和生命周期规则，比较不同社区的角色结构。

Result: 开源项目使用稳定的角色名称集合，但相同名称在不同项目中承担不同职责，不同标签描述相似功能（角色漂移）。少数参与者有时会积累技术、管理和社区职责，形成治理瓶颈。

Conclusion: 理解开源软件中的权威和职责分配对研究者和实践者都很重要。需要设计更清晰的角色、分配工作、减少领导过载，以支持更健康、可持续的社区。

Abstract: Open source software (OSS) sustainability depends not only on code contributions but also on governance structures that define who decides, who acts, and how responsibility is distributed. We lack systematic empirical evidence of how projects formally codify roles and authority in written artifacts. This paper investigates how OSS projects define and structure governance through their GOVERNANCE.md files and related documents. We analyze governance as an institutional infrastructure, a set of explicit rules that shape participation, decision rights, and community memory. We used Institutional Grammar to extract and formalize role definitions from repositories hosted on GitHub. We decompose each role into scope, privileges, obligations, and life-cycle rules to compare role structures across communities. Our results show that although OSS projects use a stable set of titles, identical titles carry different responsibilities, and different labels describe similar functions, which we call role drift. Still, we observed that a few actors sometimes accumulate technical, managerial, and community duties. %This creates the Maintainer Paradox: those who enable broad participation simultaneously become governance bottlenecks. By understanding authority and responsibilities in OSS, our findings inform researchers and practitioners on the importance of designing clearer roles, distributing work, and reducing leadership overload to support healthier and more sustainable communities.

</details>


### [228] [MobileDev-Bench: A Comprehensive Benchmark for Evaluating Language Models on Mobile Application Development](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24946)
*Moshood A. Fakorede,Krishna Upadhyay,A. B. Siddique,Umar Farooq*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: MobileDev-Bench是一个包含384个真实移动应用问题修复任务的基准测试，涵盖Android Native、React Native和Flutter平台，评估显示当前代码能力LLMs在移动开发任务上的端到端解决率仅为3.39%-5.21%，远低于其他软件工程基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM基准主要关注通用库或Web应用，而移动应用开发具有严格的平台约束、框架驱动的生命周期和复杂的平台API交互，这些特性尚未得到充分探索。移动开发任务需要处理多文件、多类型工件的协调修改，现有基准无法充分评估LLM在此领域的性能。

Method: 研究者从18个生产级移动应用中收集了384个真实开发者报告的问题，每个任务都包含可执行的测试补丁。基准涵盖Android Native(Java/Kotlin)、React Native(TypeScript)和Flutter(Dart)三大平台。通过自动化验证模型生成的修复在移动构建环境中的执行效果，评估了GPT-5.2、Claude Sonnet 4.5、Gemini Flash 2.5和Qwen3-Coder四种最先进的代码能力LLM。

Result: 基准测试显示移动修复任务具有显著复杂性：平均每个修复需要修改12.5个文件和324.9行代码，35.7%的实例需要跨多种工件类型（如源代码和清单文件）进行协调修改。所有测试的LLM端到端解决率都很低（3.39%-5.21%），远低于先前基准测试的表现。主要瓶颈在于跨多文件和多工件变更的故障定位能力不足。

Conclusion: 当前代码能力LLM在移动应用开发任务上表现不佳，特别是在处理复杂的多文件、多工件协调修改方面存在显著挑战。MobileDev-Bench填补了移动开发评估的空白，揭示了LLM在实际移动开发场景中的系统性失败模式，为未来研究提供了重要基准。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown strong performance on automated software engineering tasks, yet existing benchmarks focus primarily on general-purpose libraries or web applications, leaving mobile application development largely unexplored despite its strict platform constraints, framework-driven lifecycles, and complex platform API interactions. We introduce MobileDev-Bench, a benchmark comprising 384 real-world issue-resolution tasks collected from 18 production mobile applications spanning Android Native (Java/Kotlin), React Native (TypeScript), and Flutter (Dart). Each task pairs an authentic developer-reported issue with executable test patches, enabling fully automated validation of model-generated fixes within mobile build environments. The benchmark exhibits substantial patch complexity: fixes modify 12.5 files and 324.9 lines on average, and 35.7% of instances require coordinated changes across multiple artifact types, such as source and manifest files. Evaluation of four state-of-the-art code-capable LLMs, GPT- 5.2, Claude Sonnet 4.5, Gemini Flash 2.5, and Qwen3-Coder, yields low end-to-end resolution rates of 3.39%-5.21%, revealing significant performance gaps compared to prior benchmarks. Further analysis reveals systematic failure modes, with fault localization across multi-file and multi-artifact changes emerging as the primary bottleneck.

</details>


### [229] [Error Understanding in Program Code With LLM-DL for Multi-label Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25005)
*Md Faizul Ibne Amin,Yutaka Watanobe,Md. Mostafizer Rahman,Daniel M. Muepu,Md. Shahajada Mia*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个基于微调大语言模型的多标签编程错误分类框架，结合深度学习方法，在真实学生Python代码错误数据集上取得了良好效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编程是计算机科学和软件工程的核心技能，但识别和解决代码错误对新手和经验丰富的开发者都具有挑战性。虽然大语言模型在自然语言理解和生成任务中表现出色，但在多标签编程错误分类等特定领域复杂场景中的应用潜力尚未充分探索。

Method: 提出了多标签错误分类框架，将微调的大语言模型（CodeT5-base、GraphCodeBERT、CodeT5+、UniXcoder、RoBERTa、PLBART、CoTexT）与深度学习架构（GRU、LSTM、BiLSTM、带注意力机制的BiLSTM）结合，从真实学生编写的Python代码错误数据集中捕获语法和语义特征。使用Optuna进行超参数优化，评估了32个模型变体。

Result: CodeT5+_GRU模型表现最佳，加权F1分数为0.8243，平均准确率为91.84%，精确匹配准确率为53.78%，汉明损失为0.0816，One error为0.0708。结果证实了预训练语义编码器与高效循环解码器结合的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究为开发智能、可扩展的自动化代码反馈工具奠定了基础，在编程教育和更广泛的软件工程领域具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Programming is a core skill in computer science and software engineering (SE), yet identifying and resolving code errors remains challenging for both novice and experienced developers. While Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown remarkable capabilities in natural language understanding and generation tasks, their potential in domain-specific, complex scenarios, such as multi-label classification (MLC) of programming errors, remains underexplored. Recognizing this less-explored area, this study proposes a multi-label error classification (MLEC) framework for source code that leverages fine-tuned LLMs, including CodeT5-base, GraphCodeBERT, CodeT5+, UniXcoder, RoBERTa, PLBART, and CoTexT. These LLMs are integrated with deep learning (DL) architectures such as GRU, LSTM, BiLSTM, and BiLSTM with an additive attention mechanism (BiLSTM-A) to capture both syntactic and semantic features from a real-world student-written Python code error dataset. Extensive experiments across 32 model variants, optimized using Optuna-based hyperparameter tuning, have been evaluated using comprehensive multi-label metrics, including average accuracy, macro and weighted precision, recall, F1-score, exact match accuracy, One-error, Hamming loss, Jaccard similarity, and ROC-AUC (micro, macro, and weighted). Results show that the CodeT5+\_GRU model achieved the strongest performance, with a weighted F1-score of 0.8243, average accuracy of 91.84\%, exact match accuracy of 53.78\%, Hamming loss of 0.0816, and One error of 0.0708. These findings confirm the effectiveness of combining pretrained semantic encoders with efficient recurrent decoders. This work lays the foundation for developing intelligent, scalable tools for automated code feedback, with potential applications in programming education (PE) and broader SE domains.

</details>


### [230] [Factors Influencing the Quality of AI-Generated Code: A Synthesis of Empirical Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25146)
*Vehid Geruslu,Zulfiyya Aliyeva,Eray Tüzün*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过系统文献综述分析了影响AI生成代码质量的因素，发现代码质量受人类因素、AI系统特性和人机交互动态的共同影响，包括提示设计、任务规范和开发者专业知识等关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI辅助代码生成工具（如大语言模型）的快速采用，虽然这些工具承诺显著提高生产力，但学术界和工业界对AI生成代码的质量、可靠性和安全性日益关注，需要系统性地综合现有实证证据。

Method: 采用遵循既定指南的系统文献综述方法，结合AI辅助工作流程和人工监督，通过结构化搜索和筛选过程从主要数字图书馆中选取了24项主要研究，使用基于模式的定性证据综合进行数据提取和分析。

Result: 研究发现AI辅助开发中的代码质量受人类因素、AI系统特性和人机交互动态的共同影响，关键影响因素包括提示设计、任务规范和开发者专业知识。质量结果（如正确性、安全性、可维护性和复杂性）在不同研究中存在差异，既有改进也有风险报告。

Conclusion: AI辅助代码生成代表了软件工程中的社会技术转变，实现高质量结果既取决于技术因素也取决于人为因素。虽然前景广阔，但AI生成的代码需要仔细验证并集成到开发工作流程中。

Abstract: Context: The rapid adoption of AI-assisted code generation tools, such as large language models (LLMs), is transforming software development practices. While these tools promise significant productivity gains, concerns regarding the quality, reliability, and security of AI-generated code are increasingly reported in both academia and industry. --Objective: This study aims to systematically synthesize existing empirical evidence on the factors influencing the quality of AI-generated source code and to analyze how these factors impact software quality outcomes across different evaluation contexts. --Method: We conducted a systematic literature review (SLR) following established guidelines, supported by an AI-assisted workflow with human oversight. A total of 24 primary studies were selected through a structured search and screening process across major digital libraries. Data were extracted and analyzed using qualitative, pattern-based evidence synthesis. --Results: The findings reveal that code quality in AI-assisted development is influenced by a combination of human factors, AI system characteristics, and human AI interaction dynamics. Key influencing factors include prompt design, task specification, and developer expertise. The results also show variability in quality outcomes such as correctness, security, maintainability, and complexity across studies, with both improvements and risks reported. --Conclusion: AI-assisted code generation represents a socio-technical shift in software engineering, where achieving high-quality outcomes depends on both technological and human factors. While promising, AI-generated code requires careful validation and integration into development workflows.

</details>


### [231] [LACY: Simulating Expert Mentoring for Software Onboarding with Code Tours](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25391)
*Zeynep Begüm Kara,Aytekin İsmail,Ece Ateş,İzgi Nur Tamcı,Zehra İyigün,Selin Şirin Aslangül,Ömercan Devran,Baykal Mehmet Uçar,Eray Tüzün*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: Lacy是一个混合人机代码入门系统，通过专家引导的代码游览帮助新人理解复杂代码库，相比纯AI游览显著提高学习效果


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件组织面临新成员入门挑战：需要帮助新人导航复杂代码库、弥补文档不足、理解非自己编写的代码。专家引导虽然有效但成本高、重复性强且难以扩展

Method: Lacy采用混合人机方法，结合AI生成内容和专家策划，创建可复用的代码游览。系统包括语音转游览录制、理解测验、播客和仪表板等功能。通过与Beko的产业合作，基于20+会议、调查和访谈设计需求

Result: 在Beko生产环境部署，对3万+行代码的遗留金融系统进行对照研究。使用专家引导游览的学习者测验得分83%，而纯AI游览仅57%；学习者偏好游览而非传统自学，并报告需要更少的专家咨询。专家认为创建游览比现场引导负担更轻

Conclusion: Lacy成功解决了代码入门挑战，Beko已将其用于组织入职培训。混合人机方法在代码游览中首次结合AI生成与专家策划，显著提升学习效果并减少专家负担

Abstract: Every software organization faces the onboarding challenge: helping newcomers navigate complex codebases, compensate for insufficient documentation, and comprehend code they did not author. Expert walkthroughs are among the most effective forms of support, yet they are expensive, repetitive, and do not scale. We present Lacy, a hybrid human-AI onboarding system that captures expert mentoring in reusable code tours-to our knowledge, the first hybrid approach combining AI-generated content with expert curation in code tours. Our design is grounded in requirements derived from 20+ meetings, surveys, and interviews across a year-long industry partnership with Beko. Supporting features include Voice-to-Tour capture, comprehension quizzes, podcasts, and a dashboard. We deployed Lacy on Beko's production environment and conducted a controlled study on a legacy finance system (30K+ LOC). Learners using expert-guided tours achieved 83% quiz scores versus 57% for AI-only tours, preferred tours over traditional self-study, and reported they would need fewer expert consultations. Experts found tour creation less burdensome than live walkthroughs. Beko has since adopted Lacy for organizational onboarding, and we release our code and study instruments as a replication package.

### [232] [Quantum Circuit Repair by Gate Prioritisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25587)
*Eñaut Mendiluze Usandizaga,Thomas Laurent,Paolo Arcaini,Shaukat Ali*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: QRep是一种自动修复量子电路故障的方法，通过迭代识别和修复故障，为每个门分配可疑度分数，并优先处理最可疑的门来提高修复效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 修复有故障的量子电路具有挑战性，需要自动化解决方案。现有的量子电路修复方法效率不高，难以扩展到大型复杂电路。

Method: QRep采用迭代修复方法，为电路中的每个门分配可疑度分数，反映其故障可能性。通过在整个电路中统一应用补丁，并优先处理最可疑的门来缩小搜索空间，提高修复效率。

Result: 在40个真实和合成的故障电路上评估QRep，完全修复了70%的电路。对于剩余电路，实际故障门被排在前44%最可疑的门中。相比两种基线方法，QRep能够扩展到更大更复杂的电路（最多13个量子比特）。

Conclusion: QRep在量子电路故障定位和修复方面表现出有效性，能够扩展到较大规模的量子电路，为量子计算中的自动化电路修复提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: Repairing faulty quantum circuits is challenging and requires automated solutions. We present QRep, an automated repair approach that iteratively identifies and repairs faults in a circuit. QRep uniformly applies patches across the circuit and assigns each gate a suspiciousness score, reflecting its likelihood of being faulty. It then narrows the search space by prioritising the most suspicious gates in subsequent iterations, increasing the repair efficiency. We evaluated QRep on 40 (real and synthetic) faulty circuits. QRep completely repaired 70% of them, and for the remaining circuits, the actual faulty gate was ranked within the top 44% most suspicious gates, demonstrating the effectiveness of QRep in fault localisation. Compared with two baseline approaches, QRep scales to larger and more complex circuits, up to 13 qubits.

</details>


### [233] [SHAPR: Operationalising Human-AI Collaborative Research Through Structured Knowledge Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25660)
*Ka Ching Chan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: SHAPR框架将人本决策与AI辅助能力结合，通过结构化、可追溯、知识生成的方法实现AI辅助研究实践，支持透明、可复现的研究工作流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然之前的研究提出了SHAPR作为概念框架，但缺乏具体的操作化方法。本文旨在将SHAPR转化为结构化、可追溯、知识生成的研究实践方法，以支持AI辅助环境下的严谨、透明、可复现研究。

Method: 提出一套相互关联的模型：研究活动通过迭代循环（探索-构建-使用-评估-学习）组织；人工制品通过开发和使用演进；经验证据转化为概念知识。核心是结构化知识单元（SKUs），提供模块化、可重用的实践洞察表示。框架引入证据和可追溯性作为跨领域机制，连接人类决策、AI辅助开发和人工制品演进。

Result: SHAPR被定位为AI可执行的研究框架，其结构化流程和文档可由生成式AI系统解释以指导研究工作流。同时支持AI参与的连续性，允许研究人员在不同情境下平衡控制、学习和自动化。框架被概念化为集成研究系统，结合LLM工作空间、开发环境、云存储和版本控制。

Conclusion: SHAPR为在AI辅助环境中进行严谨、透明、可复现的研究提供了实践和理论基础，有助于发展可扩展且方法学健全的研究实践，促进知识积累和系统化改进。

Abstract: SHAPR (Solo Human-Centred and AI-Assisted Practice) is a framework for research software development that integrates human-centred decision-making with AI-assisted capabilities. While prior work introduced SHAPR as a conceptual framework, this paper focuses on its operationalisation as a structured, traceable, and knowledge-generating approach to AI-assisted research practice. We present a set of interconnected models describing how research activities are organised through iterative cycles (Explore-Build-Use-Evaluate-Learn), how artefacts evolve through development and use, and how empirical evidence is transformed into conceptual knowledge. Central to this process are Structured Knowledge Units (SKUs), which provide modular and reusable representations of insights derived from practice, supporting knowledge accumulation across cycles. The framework introduces evidence and traceability as a cross-cutting mechanism linking human decisions, AI-assisted development, and artefact evolution to enable transparency, reproducibility, and systematic refinement. SHAPR is also positioned as an AI-executable research framework, as its structured processes and documentation can be interpreted by generative AI systems to guide research workflows. Simultaneously, SHAPR supports a continuum of AI involvement, allowing researchers to balance control, learning, and automation across different contexts. Beyond individual workflows, SHAPR is conceptualised as an integrated research system combining LLM workspaces, development environments, cloud storage, and version control to support scalable, knowledge-centred research practices. Overall, SHAPR provides a practical and theoretically grounded foundation for conducting rigorous, transparent, and reproducible research in AI-assisted environments, contributing to the development of scalable and methodologically sound research practices.

</details>
